Reasonable flavor name length\n                flavor_name = title_text\n                print(f"Potential flavor name from title: {flavor_name}")\n                break\n        \n        # Look for dates or years\n        import re\n        year_matches = re.findall(r\'\\b(19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})\\b\', container_text)\n        dates_found = list(set(year_matches))  # Remove duplicates\n        \n        if dates_found:\n            print(f"Years/dates found: {dates_found}")\n        \n        # Look for images within the container\n        images = container.find_all(\'img\') if hasattr(container, \'find_all\') else []\n        image_urls = []\n        \n        for img in images:\n            img_src = img.get(\'src\', \'\') or img.get(\'data-src\', \'\')\n            if img_src:\n                # Store flavor data if we have meaningful information\n        if flavor_name or dates_found or image_urls:\n            flavor_data = {\n                \'container_index\': i,\n                \'flavor_name\': flavor_name,\n                \'years_found\': dates_found,\n                \'images\': image_urls,\n                \'container_text\': container_text[:500]  # First 500 chars\n            }\n            flavors_data.append(flavor_data)\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 4: FLAVOR DATA SUMMARY ===\\n")\n    print(f"Flavors with meaningful data extracted: {len(flavors_data)}")\n    \n    # Look for links that might be flavor-related\n        if any(keyword in href.lower() for keyword in [\'flavor\', \'graveyard\', \'discontinued\']):\n            flavor_links.append({\n                \'href\': href,\n                \'text\': link_text,\n                \'full_url\': href if href.startswith(\'http\') else f\'https://www.benjerry.com{href}\' if href.startswith(\'/\') else f\'https://www.benjerry.com/flavors/{href}\'\n            })\n    \n    print(f"Found {len(flavor_links)} potentially flavor-related links:")\n    for i, link in enumerate(flavor_links[:10], 1):  # Split text into paragraphs and sentences\n    paragraphs = page_text.split(\'\\n\')\n    \n    # Look for year patterns (1970s-2020s)\n    year_pattern = r\'\\b(19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)\\b\'\n    date_pattern = r\'\\b(19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)[-â€“â€”](19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)\\b\'  # Date ranges\n    \n    potential_flavors = []\n    \n    for i, paragraph in enumerate(paragraphs):\n        paragraph_clean = paragraph.strip()\n        if len(paragraph_clean) < 10 or len(paragraph_clean) > 500:  # Skip very short or very long paragraphs\n            continue\n            \n        # Check if paragraph contains years\n        years_found = re.findall(year_pattern, paragraph_clean)\n        date_ranges = re.findall(date_pattern, paragraph_clean)\n        \n        if years_found or date_ranges:\n            # This paragraph might contain flavor information\n            potential_flavors.append({\n                \'paragraph_index\': i,\n                \'text\': paragraph_clean,\n                \'years\': years_found,\n                \'date_ranges\': date_ranges\n            })\n    \n    print(f"Found {len(potential_flavors)} paragraphs with date information:")\n    \n    for i, flavor_info in enumerate(potential_flavors[:10], 1):  # Years: {flavor_info[\'years\']} | Ranges: {flavor_info[\'date_ranges\']}")\n        print(f"   Text: {flavor_info[\'text\'][:150]}{\'...\' if len(flavor_info[\'text\']) > 150 else \'\'}")\n    \n    # Approach 4: Look for images that might be headstones\n    print("\\n=== STEP 4: SEARCHING FOR HEADSTONE IMAGES ===\\n")\n    \n    all_images = soup.find_all(\'img\')\n    print(f"Total images found on page: {len(all_images)}")\n    \n    headstone_images = []\n    \n    for img in all_images:\n        img_src = img.get(\'src\', \'\') or img.get(\'data-src\', \'\') or img.get(\'data-lazy-src\', \'\')\n        img_alt = img.get(\'alt\', \'\')\n        img_title = img.get(\'title\', \'\')\n        \n        if img_src:\n            # Convert relative URLs to absolute\n            if img_src.startswith(\'//\'):\n                img_src = \'https:\' + img_src\n            elif img_src.startswith(\'/\'):\n                img_src = \'https://www.benjerry.com\' + img_src\n            elif not img_src.startswith(\'http\'):\n                img_src = \'https://www.benjerry.com/\' + img_src\n            \n            # Check if this might be a headstone image\n            headstone_keywords = [\'headstone\', \'graveyard\', \'grave\', \'tombstone\', \'rip\', \'flavor\']\n            \n            img_context = f"{img_src} {img_alt} {img_title}".lower()\n            \n            if any(keyword in img_context for keyword in headstone_keywords) or \'graveyard\' in img_src.lower():\n                headstone_images.append({\n                    \'src\': img_src,\n                    \'alt\': img_alt,\n                    \'title\': img_title,\n                    \'context_score\': sum(1 for keyword in headstone_keywords if keyword in img_context)\n                })\n    \n    print(f"Found {len(headstone_images)} potentially relevant images:")\n    \n    for i, img in enumerate(headstone_images, 1):\n        print(f"\\n{i}. Source: {img[\'src\']}")\n        print(f"   Alt text: {img[\'alt\']}")\n        print(f"   Title: {img[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"   Relevance score: {img[\'context_score\']}")\n    \n    # Save all extracted data\n    extraction_data = {\n        \'extraction_date\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'source_url\': graveyard_url,\n        \'page_title\': page_title,\n        \'content_stats\': {\n            \'page_length\': len(page_text),\n            \'flavor_mentions\': flavor_mentions,\n            \'graveyard_mentions\': graveyard_mentions,\n            \'discontinued_mentions\': discontinued_mentions\n        },\n        \'containers_found\': len(unique_containers),\n        \'flavor_links\': flavor_links,\n        \'potential_flavors_with_dates\': potential_flavors,\n        \'headstone_images\': headstone_images,\n        \'total_images\': len(all_images)\n    }\n    \n    extraction_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_graveyard_extraction_requests.json\')\n    with open(extraction_file, \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(extraction_data, f, indent=2)\n    \n    print(f"\\nâœ“ Complete extraction data saved to: {extraction_file}")\n    \n    #     "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport re\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nprint("=== ANALYZING EXISTING BEN & JERRY\'S GRAVEYARD DATA ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Parse existing HTML file to find oldest flavor and headstone photos")\nprint("Strategy: Analyze workspace files, extract flavor data, identify oldest flavor\\n")\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n# First, let\'s inspect the existing files to understand their structure\nprint("=== STEP 1: INSPECTING EXISTING WORKSPACE FILES ===\\n")\n\nworkspace_files = os.listdir(workspace_dir)\nprint(f"Files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}")\n\nfor file in workspace_files:\n    file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file)\n    file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n    print(f"  - {file} ({file_size:,} bytes)")\n\n# Inspect the JSON file structure first (as recommended)\njson_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_flavors_initial_extraction.json\')\nif os.path.exists(json_file):\n    print(f"\\n=== INSPECTING JSON FILE STRUCTURE ===\\n")\n    print(f"Reading: {json_file}")\n    \n    with open(json_file, \'r\') as f:\n        json_content = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"JSON file content length: {len(json_content)} characters")\n    print(f"JSON content preview: {json_content}")\n    \n    try:\n        json_data = json.loads(json_content)\n        print(f"\\nJSON structure:")\n        for key, value in json_data.items():\n            if isinstance(value, list):\n                print(f"  {key}: List with {len(value)} items")\n            elif isinstance(value, dict):\n                print(f"  {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys")\n            else:\n                print(f"  {key}: {value}")\n        \n        # If there\'s flavor data, show a sample\n        if \'flavors_data\' in json_data and json_data[\'flavors_data\']:\n            print(f"\\nSample flavor data structure:")\n            sample_flavor = json_data[\'flavors_data\'][0]\n            for key, value in sample_flavor.items():\n                print(f"    {key}: {type(value).__name__} - {str(value)[:100]}{\'...\' if len(str(value)) > 100 else \'\'}")\n    \n    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n        print(f"JSON parsing error: {e}")\n        print("File may be corrupted or incomplete")\nelse:\n    print(f"JSON file not found: {json_file}")\n\n# Now analyze the main HTML file\nhtml_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_graveyard_page.html\')\nif os.path.exists(html_file):\n    print(f"\\n=== ANALYZING HTML FILE ===\\n")\n    print(f"Reading: {html_file}")\n    \n    with open(html_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        html_content = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"HTML file length: {len(html_content):,} characters")\n    \n    # Parse with BeautifulSoup\n    print(f"Parsing HTML content...")\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Get page title\n    page_title = soup.title.get_text(strip=True) if soup.title else \'No title found\'\n    print(f"Page title: {page_title}")\n    \n    # Basic content analysis\n    page_text = soup.get_text()\n    print(f"Total text length: {len(page_text):,} characters")\n    \n    flavor_mentions = page_text.lower().count(\'flavor\')\n    graveyard_mentions = page_text.lower().count(\'graveyard\')\n    discontinued_mentions = page_text.lower().count(\'discontinued\')\n    \n    print(f"Content analysis:")\n    print(f"  \'Flavor\' mentions: {flavor_mentions}")\n    print(f"  \'Graveyard\' mentions: {graveyard_mentions}")\n    print(f"  \'Discontinued\' mentions: {discontinued_mentions}")\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 2: SEARCHING FOR FLAVOR CONTAINERS ===\\n")\n    \n    # Try multiple approaches to find flavor information\n    \n    # Approach 1: Look for common container patterns\n    container_selectors = [\n        \'.flavor-card\',\n        \'.flavor-item\', \n        \'.graveyard-item\',\n        \'.flavor\',\n        \'.product-card\',\n        \'.card\',\n        \'.item\',\n        \'[data-flavor]\',\n        \'.graveyard-flavor\',\n        \'.discontinued-flavor\',\n        \'div[class*="flavor"]\',\n        \'div[class*="graveyard"]\',\n        \'div[class*="card"]\'\n    ]\n    \n    print("Searching for flavor containers using CSS selectors...")\n    all_containers = []\n    \n    for selector in container_selectors:\n        elements = soup.select(selector)\n        if elements:\n            print(f"  Found {len(elements)} elements with selector \'{selector}\'")\n            all_containers.extend(elements)\n        else:\n            print(f"  No elements found with selector \'{selector}\'")\n    \n    # Remove duplicates\n    unique_containers = list(set(all_containers))\n    print(f"\\nTotal unique containers found: {len(unique_containers)}")\n    \n    # Approach 2: Look for any divs or sections that might contain flavor information\n    print(f"\\nSearching for divs and sections with flavor-related content...")\n    \n    all_divs = soup.find_all([\'div\', \'section\', \'article\'])\n    flavor_divs = []\n    \n    for div in all_divs:\n        div_text = div.get_text(strip=True)\n        div_classes = \' \'.join(div.get(\'class\', []))\n        div_id = div.get(\'id\', \'\')\n        \n        # Check if this div contains flavor-related content\n        combined_text = f"{div_text} {div_classes} {div_id}".lower()\n        \n        if any(keyword in combined_text for keyword in [\'flavor\', \'graveyard\', \'discontinued\']) and len(div_text) > 20:\n            flavor_divs.append({\n                \'element\': div,\n                \'text\': div_text[:200] + (\'...\' if len(div_text) > 200 else \'\'),\n                \'classes\': div_classes,\n                \'id\': div_id,\n                \'text_length\': len(div_text)\n            })\n    \n    print(f"Found {len(flavor_divs)} divs with flavor-related content")\n    \n    # Sort by text length (longer content might be more relevant)\n    flavor_divs.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'text_length\'], reverse=True)\n    \n    print(f"\\nTop 10 flavor-related divs by content length:")\n    for i, div_info in enumerate(flavor_divs[:10], 1):\n        print(f"\\n{i}. Length: {div_info[\'text_length\']:,} chars")\n        print(f"   Classes: {div_info[\'classes\']}")\n        print(f"   ID: {div_info[\'id\']}")\n        print(f"   Text preview: {div_info[\'text\']}")\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 3: SEARCHING FOR IMAGES (HEADSTONES) ===\\n")\n    \n    # Find all images\n    all_images = soup.find_all(\'img\')\n    print(f"Total images found: {len(all_images)}")\n    \n    headstone_images = []\n    \n    for img in all_images:\n        img_src = img.get(\'src\', \'\') or img.get(\'data-src\', \'\') or img.get(\'data-lazy-src\', \'\')\n        img_alt = img.get(\'alt\', \'\')\n        img_title = img.get(\'title\', \'\')\n        img_class = \' \'.join(img.get(\'class\', []))\n        \n        if img_src:\n            # Convert relative URLs to absolute\n            if img_src.startswith(\'//\'):\n                img_src = \'https:\' + img_src\n            elif img_src.startswith(\'/\'):\n                img_src = \'https://www.benjerry.com\' + img_src\n            elif not img_src.startswith(\'http\'):\n                img_src = \'https://www.benjerry.com/\' + img_src\n            \n            # Check relevance for headstone/graveyard images\n            img_context = f"{img_src} {img_alt} {img_title} {img_class}".lower()\n            \n            relevance_keywords = [\'headstone\', \'graveyard\', \'grave\', \'tombstone\', \'rip\', \'flavor\', \'discontinued\']\n            relevance_score = sum(1 for keyword in relevance_keywords if keyword in img_context)\n            \n            if relevance_score > 0 or \'graveyard\' in img_src.lower() or \'flavor\' in img_src.lower():\n                headstone_images.append({\n                    \'src\': img_src,\n                    \'alt\': img_alt,\n                    \'title\': img_title,\n                    \'class\': img_class,\n                    \'relevance_score\': relevance_score,\n                    \'context\': img_context\n                })\n    \n    # Sort by relevance score\n    headstone_images.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'relevance_score\'], reverse=True)\n    \n    print(f"Found {len(headstone_images)} potentially relevant images:")\n    \n    for i, img in enumerate(headstone_images[:15], 1):  # Show top 15\n        print(f"\\n{i}. Relevance score: {img[\'relevance_score\']}")\n        print(f"   Source: {img[\'src\']}")\n        print(f"   Alt text: {img[\'alt\']}")\n        print(f"   Title: {img[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"   Class: {img[\'class\']}")\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 4: SEARCHING FOR FLAVOR NAMES AND DATES ===\\n")\n    \n    # Look for text patterns that indicate flavor names with dates\n    year_pattern = r\'\\b(19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)\\b\'  # 1970-2029\n    date_range_pattern = r\'\\b(19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)[-â€“â€”](19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)\\b\'  # Date ranges\n    \n    # Split page text into meaningful chunks\n    paragraphs = [p.strip() for p in page_text.split(\'\\n\') if p.strip()]\n    \n    flavors_with_dates = []\n    \n    for paragraph in paragraphs:\n        if len(paragraph) < 10 or len(paragraph) > 1000:  # Skip very short or very long paragraphs\n            continue\n        \n        # Check if paragraph contains years\n        years_found = re.findall(year_pattern, paragraph)\n        date_ranges = re.findall(date_range_pattern, paragraph)\n        \n        if years_found or date_ranges:\n            # This might be a flavor with date information\n            flavors_with_dates.append({\n                \'text\': paragraph,\n                \'years\': list(set(years_found)),  # Remove duplicates\n                \'date_ranges\': date_ranges,\n                \'earliest_year\': min([int(y) for y in years_found]) if years_found else None\n            })\n    \n    print(f"Found {len(flavors_with_dates)} text sections with date information")\n    \n    # Sort by earliest year to find the oldest\n    flavors_with_dates_sorted = [f for f in flavors_with_dates if f[\'earliest_year\']]\n    flavors_with_dates_sorted.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'earliest_year\'])\n    \n    print(f"\\nTop 15 sections by earliest year (potential oldest flavors):")\n    for i, flavor_info in enumerate(flavors_with_dates_sorted[:15], 1):\n        print(f"\\n{i}. Earliest year: {flavor_info[\'earliest_year\']}")\n        print(f"   All years: {flavor_info[\'years\']}")\n        print(f"   Date ranges: {flavor_info[\'date_ranges\']}")\n        print(f"   Text: {flavor_info[\'text\'][:200]}{\'...\' if len(flavor_info[\'text\']) > 200 else \'\'}")\n    \n    # Save comprehensive analysis\n    analysis_data = {\n        \'analysis_date\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'source_file\': html_file,\n        \'page_title\': page_title,\n        \'content_stats\': {\n            \'html_length\': len(html_content),\n            \'text_length\': len(page_text),\n            \'flavor_mentions\': flavor_mentions,\n            \'graveyard_mentions\': graveyard_mentions,\n            \'discontinued_mentions\': discontinued_mentions\n        },\n        \'containers_found\': len(unique_containers),\n        \'flavor_divs_found\': len(flavor_divs),\n        \'total_images\': len(all_images),\n        \'relevant_images\': len(headstone_images),\n        \'flavors_with_dates\': len(flavors_with_dates),\n        \'top_flavor_divs\': flavor_divs[:10],  # Top 10 by content length\n        \'top_headstone_images\': headstone_images[:10],  # Top 10 by relevance\n        \'oldest_flavors_candidates\': flavors_with_dates_sorted[:10]  # Top 10 oldest\n    }\n    \n    analysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_comprehensive_analysis.json\')\n    with open(analysis_file, \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(analysis_data, f, indent=2, default=str)  # default=str to handle any non-serializable objects\n    \n    print(f"\\nâœ“ Comprehensive analysis saved to: {analysis_file}")\n    \n    # Summary and next steps\n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 5: ANALYSIS SUMMARY ===\\n")\n    print(f"âœ“ Successfully parsed Ben & Jerry\'s Graveyard HTML ({len(html_content):,} chars)")\n    print(f"âœ“ Found {len(flavor_divs)} flavor-related content sections")\n    print(f"âœ“ Located {len(headstone_images)} potentially relevant images")\n    print(f"âœ“ Identified {len(flavors_with_dates)} text sections with date information")\n    \n    if flavors_with_dates_sorted:\n        oldest_candidate = flavors_with_dates_sorted[0]\n        print(f"\\nðŸŽ¯ OLDEST FLAVOR CANDIDATE IDENTIFIED:")\n        print(f"   Earliest year: {oldest_candidate[\'earliest_year\']}")\n        print(f"   Years mentioned: {oldest_candidate[\'years\']}")\n        print(f"   Text preview: {oldest_candidate[\'text\'][:300]}...")\n        \n        print(f"\\nðŸ“‹ NEXT STEPS:")\n        print(f"   1. Extract flavor name and rhyme text from background headstone")\n    else:\n        print(f"\\nâš  No clear oldest flavor identified - may need refined analysis")\n        print(f"Recommendation: Examine flavor divs and images more closely")\n\nelse:\n    print(f"HTML file not found: {html_file}")\n    print(f"Cannot proceed with analysis without the graveyard page content")\n\nprint(f"\\n=== COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\\n")\nprint(f"Ready to proceed with oldest flavor identification and headstone image analysis")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport re\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nprint("=== REFINED FLAVOR DATE EXTRACTION FROM ACCORDION SECTIONS ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Extract actual flavor names and discontinuation dates from accordion content")\nprint("Strategy: Focus on the 7,640-character accordion sections that contain flavor details\\n")\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n# First inspect the comprehensive analysis file structure\nanalysis_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_comprehensive_analysis.json\')\nif os.path.exists(analysis_file):\n    print("=== STEP 1: INSPECTING COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS FILE STRUCTURE ===\\n")\n    \n    with open(analysis_file, \'r\') as f:\n        analysis_content = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"Analysis file size: {len(analysis_content):,} characters")\n    \n    try:\n        analysis_data = json.loads(analysis_content)\n        print("\\nAnalysis file structure:")\n        for key, value in analysis_data.items():\n            if isinstance(value, list):\n                print(f"  {key}: List with {len(value)} items")\n            elif isinstance(value, dict):\n                print(f"  {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys")\n            else:\n                print(f"  {key}: {value}")\n        \n        # Examine the top flavor divs structure\n        if \'top_flavor_divs\' in analysis_data:\n            print(f"\\nTop flavor divs structure (first item):")\n            if analysis_data[\'top_flavor_divs\']:\n                first_div = analysis_data[\'top_flavor_divs\'][0]\n                for key, value in first_div.items():\n                    if key == \'text\':\n                        print(f"  {key}: {len(str(value))} characters")\n                    else:\n                        print(f"  {key}: {value}")\n    \n    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n        print(f"JSON parsing error: {e}")\nelse:\n    print(f"Analysis file not found: {analysis_file}")\n\n# Now analyze the HTML file directly, focusing on accordion sections\nhtml_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_graveyard_page.html\')\nif os.path.exists(html_file):\n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 2: FOCUSED ANALYSIS OF ACCORDION SECTIONS ===\\n")\n    \n    with open(html_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        html_content = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"HTML file length: {len(html_content):,} characters")\n    \n    # Parse with BeautifulSoup\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Look specifically for accordion elements and their content\n    print("Searching for accordion elements...")\n    \n    accordion_elements = soup.find_all([\'div\'], class_=lambda x: x and \'accordion\' in \' \'.join(x))\n    print(f"Found {len(accordion_elements)} accordion elements")\n    \n    # Also look for collapse elements that contain flavor information\n    collapse_elements = soup.find_all([\'div\'], class_=lambda x: x and \'collapse\' in \' \'.join(x))\n    print(f"Found {len(collapse_elements)} collapse elements")\n    \n    # Combine and analyze all potential flavor containers\n    flavor_containers = accordion_elements + collapse_elements\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 3: EXTRACTING FLAVOR NAMES AND DATES FROM CONTAINERS ===\\n")\n    \n    extracted_flavors = []\n    \n    for i, container in enumerate(flavor_containers, 1):\n        container_text = container.get_text(strip=True)\n        container_classes = \' \'.join(container.get(\'class\', []))\n        container_id = container.get(\'id\', \'\')\n        \n        print(f"\\nContainer {i}:")\n        print(f"  Classes: {container_classes}")\n        print(f"  ID: {container_id}")\n        print(f"  Text length: {len(container_text):,} characters")\n        \n        if len(container_text) > 100:  # Focus on containers with substantial content\n            print(f"  Text preview: {container_text[:200]}...")\n            \n            # Look for flavor name patterns (usually at the beginning)\n            lines = container_text.split(\'\\n\')\n            first_meaningful_line = None\n            \n            for line in lines:\n                line_clean = line.strip()\n                if len(line_clean) > 3 and not line_clean.lower().startswith((\'skip\', \'search\', \'suggestions\')):\n                    first_meaningful_line = line_clean\n                    break\n            \n            if first_meaningful_line:\n                print(f"  First meaningful line (potential flavor name): {first_meaningful_line}")\n            \n            # Extract date patterns with more comprehensive regex\n            date_patterns = [\n                r\'(\\d{4})[-â€“â€”](\\d{4})\',  # 1993-2001\n                r\'(\\d{4})\\s*[-â€“â€”]\\s*(\\d{4})\',  # 1993 - 2001\n                r\'\\b(19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})[-â€“â€”](19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})\\b\',  # More specific year ranges\n                r\'\\b(19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})\\s*[-â€“â€”]\\s*(19\\d{2}|20\\d{2})\\b\'  # With spaces\n            ]\n            \n            dates_found = []\n            for pattern in date_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, container_text)\n                dates_found.extend(matches)\n            \n            # Also look for individual years\n            individual_years = re.findall(r\'\\b(19[7-9]\\d|20[0-2]\\d)\\b\', container_text)\n            \n            if dates_found or individual_years:\n                print(f"  Date ranges found: {dates_found}")\n                print(f"  Individual years found: {individual_years}")\n                \n                # Determine the earliest year for this flavor\n                all_years = []\n                for date_range in dates_found:\n                    all_years.extend([int(date_range[0]), int(date_range[1])])\n                all_years.extend([int(year) for year in individual_years])\n                \n                if all_years:\n                    earliest_year = min(all_years)\n                    latest_year = max(all_years)\n                    \n                    # Try to extract the flavor name more precisely\n                    flavor_name = None\n                    \n                    # Look for text before the first date\n                    text_before_date = container_text\n                    for pattern in date_patterns + [r\'\\b19\\d{2}\\b\', r\'\\b20\\d{2}\\b\']:\n                        match = re.search(pattern, text_before_date)\n                        if match:\n                            text_before_date = text_before_date[:match.start()].strip()\n                            break\n                    \n                    # Clean up the potential flavor name\n                    potential_names = [line.strip() for line in text_before_date.split(\'\\n\') if line.strip()]\n                    \n                    # Find the most likely flavor name (usually short and meaningful)\n                    for name in potential_names:\n                        if 5 <= len(name) <= 50 and not any(skip_word in name.lower() for skip_word in [\'skip\', \'search\', \'flavor graveyard\', \'ben & jerry\', \'ice cream\']):\n                            flavor_name = name\n                            break\n                    \n                    if not flavor_name and potential_names:\n                        flavor_name = potential_names[0]  # Fallback to first line\n                    \n                    extracted_flavors.append({\n                        \'container_index\': i,\n                        \'flavor_name\': flavor_name,\n                        \'earliest_year\': earliest_year,\n                        \'latest_year\': latest_year,\n                        \'date_ranges\': dates_found,\n                        \'individual_years\': individual_years,\n                        \'container_classes\': container_classes,\n                        \'container_text_preview\': container_text[:500]\n                    })\n                    \n                    print(f"  *** FLAVOR EXTRACTED ***")\n                    print(f"      Name: {flavor_name}")\n                    print(f"      Earliest year: {earliest_year}")\n                    print(f"      Latest year: {latest_year}")\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 4: SORTING FLAVORS BY AGE TO FIND THE OLDEST ===\\n")\n    \n    # Sort by earliest year to find the true oldest flavor\n    extracted_flavors.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'earliest_year\'])\n    \n    print(f"Total flavors extracted: {len(extracted_flavors)}")\n    print(f"\\nTop 15 oldest flavors:")\n    \n    for i, flavor in enumerate(extracted_flavors[:15], 1):\n        print(f"\\n{i}. {flavor[\'flavor_name\'] or \'Unknown Name\'}")\n        print(f"   Years: {flavor[\'earliest_year\']} - {flavor[\'latest_year\']}")\n        print(f"   Date ranges: {flavor[\'date_ranges\']}")\n        print(f"   Container classes: {flavor[\'container_classes\']}")\n    \n    if extracted_flavors:\n        oldest_flavor = extracted_flavors[0]\n        print(f"\\nðŸŽ¯ OLDEST FLAVOR IDENTIFIED:")\n        print(f"   Name: {oldest_flavor[\'flavor_name\']}")\n        print(f"   Years: {oldest_flavor[\'earliest_year\']} - {oldest_flavor[\'latest_year\']}")\n        print(f"   Date ranges: {oldest_flavor[\'date_ranges\']}")\n        \n        print(f"\\n=== STEP 5: FINDING HEADSTONE IMAGE FOR OLDEST FLAVOR ===\\n")\n        \n        # Load the headstone images from previous analysis\n        if \'analysis_data\' in locals() and \'top_headstone_images\' in analysis_data:\n            headstone_images = analysis_data[\'top_headstone_images\']\n            print(f"Available headstone images: {len(headstone_images)}")\n            \n            # Try to match the oldest flavor name with a headstone image\n            oldest_flavor_name = oldest_flavor[\'flavor_name\'] or \'\'\n            matching_headstones = []\n            \n            for img in headstone_images:\n                img_alt = img.get(\'alt\', \'\').lower()\n                img_src = img.get(\'src\', \'\').lower()\n                \n                # Check if the flavor name appears in the image alt text or filename\n                if oldest_flavor_name:\n                    flavor_words = oldest_flavor_name.lower().split()\n                    if any(word in img_alt or word in img_src for word in flavor_words if len(word) > 3):\n                        matching_headstones.append(img)\n            \n            if matching_headstones:\n                print(f"Found {len(matching_headstones)} potentially matching headstone images:")\n                for i, img in enumerate(matching_headstones, 1):\n                    print(f"\\n{i}. {img[\'src\']}")\n                    print(f"   Alt text: {img[\'alt\']}")\n                    print(f"   Relevance score: {img.get(\'relevance_score\', 0)}")\n                \n                best_match = matching_headstones[0]\n                print(f"\\nâœ“ BEST MATCHING HEADSTONE IMAGE:")\n                print(f"   URL: {best_match[\'src\']}")\n                print(f"   Alt text: {best_match[\'alt\']}")\n            else:\n                print(f"No direct matches found for \'{oldest_flavor_name}\'")\n                print(f"Will need to examine all headstone images manually")\n                \n                # Show all available headstone images for manual inspection\n                print(f"\\nAll available headstone images:")\n                for i, img in enumerate(headstone_images[:10], 1):\n                    print(f"\\n{i}. {img[\'alt\']}")\n                    print(f"   URL: {img[\'src\']}")\n    \n    # Save the refined flavor extraction results\n    refined_results = {\n        \'analysis_date\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n        \'extraction_method\': \'focused_accordion_analysis\',\n        \'total_flavors_extracted\': len(extracted_flavors),\n        \'oldest_flavor\': oldest_flavor if extracted_flavors else None,\n        \'all_flavors_by_age\': extracted_flavors,\n        \'next_steps\': [\n            \'Download the oldest flavor headstone image\',\n            \'Analyze the image for background headstones\',\n            \'Extract flavor name and rhyme from background headstone\',\n            \'Identify the last line of the background headstone rhyme\'\n        ]\n    }\n    \n    refined_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_refined_flavor_extraction.json\')\n    with open(refined_file, \'w\') as f:\n        json.dump(refined_results, f, indent=2)\n    \n    print(f"\\nâœ“ Refined flavor extraction results saved to: {refined_file}")\n    \nelse:\n    print(f"HTML file not found: {html_file}")\n\nprint(f"\\n=== REFINED FLAVOR EXTRACTION COMPLETE ===\\n")\nprint(f"Next: Download and analyze the oldest flavor\'s headstone image for background details")',

Skip empty lines and very short lines\n                    if len(line_clean) < 5:\n                        continue\n                    \n                    # Look for date patterns in this line\n                    date_match = re.search(date_pattern, line_clean)\n                    \n                    if date_match:\n                        start_year = int(date_match.group(1))\n                        end_year = int(date_match.group(2))\n                        \n                        # The flavor name should be the text before the date\n                        text_before_date = line_clean[:date_match.start()].strip()\n                        \n                        # Clean up the flavor name\n                        if text_before_date and len(text_before_date) < 100:  # Reasonable flavor name length\n                            flavor_name = text_before_date\n                            \n                            # Look for the description and rhyme in subsequent lines\n                            flavor_info = {\n                                \'name\': flavor_name,\n                                \'start_year\': start_year,\n                                \'end_year\': end_year,\n                                \'date_range\': f\'{start_year}-{end_year}\',\n                                \'earliest_year\': start_year\n                            }\n                            \n                            extracted_flavors.append(flavor_info)\n                            \n                            print(f"  Found: {flavor_name} ({start_year}-{end_year})")\n                \n                # Check if this is the accordion div\n                    if \'accordion\' in div[\'classes\']:\n                        print(f"  *** FOUND ACCORDION DIV ***")\n                        accordion_div = div\n                        accordion_div_index = i\n                        break\n            \n            if accordion_div and \'text\' in accordion_div:\n                print(f"\\n=== STEP 2: PARSING ACCORDION CONTENT FOR ALL FLAVORS ===\\n")\n                \n                accordion_text = accordion_div[\'text\']\n                print(f"Accordion text length: {len(accordion_text):,} characters")\n                print(f"Text preview: {accordion_text[:300]}...")\n                \n                # Parse the accordion HTML content\n                soup = BeautifulSoup(accordion_text, \'html.parser\')\n                \n                # Look for accordion items\n                accordion_items = soup.find_all(\'li\', class_=\'accordion-item\')\n                print(f"\\nFound {len(accordion_items)} accordion items")\n                \n                if len(accordion_items) == 0:\n                    # Try to extract flavor data from text patterns\n                    # Look for flavor name + date pattern\n                    flavor_pattern = r\'([A-Za-z\\s&\\\'!]+?)(\\d{4})[-â€“â€”](\\d{4})\'\n                    \n                    matches = re.findall(flavor_pattern, accordion_text)\n                    print(f"Found {len(matches)} flavor name + date patterns")\n                    \n                    extracted_flavors = []\n                    \n                    for match in matches:\n                        flavor_name = match[0].strip()\n                        start_year = int(match[1])\n                        end_year = int(match[2])\n                        \n                        # Clean up flavor name\n                        flavor_name = re.sub(r\'^(Skip to|Search|Flavor Graveyard)\', \'\', flavor_name).strip()\n                        \n                        # Filter out invalid names\n                        if len(flavor_name) > 3 and len(flavor_name) < 50 and not any(skip in flavor_name.lower() for skip in [\'skip\', \'search\', \'suggestions\', \'ice cream flavors\']):\n                            flavor_info = {\n                                \'name\': flavor_name,\n                                \'start_year\': start_year,\n                                \'end_year\': end_year,\n                                \'date_range\': f\'{start_year}-{end_year}\',\n                                \'earliest_year\': start_year\n                            }\n                            \n                            extracted_flavors.append(flavor_info)\n                            print(f"  Extracted: {flavor_name} ({start_year}-{end_year})")\n                \n                else:\n                    # Process accordion items normally\n                    extracted_flavors = []\n                    \n                    for item_idx, item in enumerate(accordion_items, 1):\n                        #     "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport re\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nprint("=== DIRECT HTML PARSING TO EXTRACT ALL GRAVEYARD FLAVORS ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Parse the original HTML file directly to extract all flavor names and dates")\nprint("Strategy: Access ben_jerrys_graveyard_page.html and parse accordion structure directly\\n")\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nworkspace_dir = \'workspace\'\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n# Access the original HTML file directly\nhtml_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_graveyard_page.html\')\nif os.path.exists(html_file):\n    print("=== STEP 1: READING ORIGINAL HTML FILE ===\\n")\n    \n    with open(html_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        html_content = f.read()\n    \n    print(f"HTML file size: {len(html_content):,} characters")\n    \n    # Parse the HTML with BeautifulSoup\n    print("\\nParsing HTML content with BeautifulSoup...")\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Look for the main accordion container\n    accordion_container = soup.find(\'div\', class_=\'accordion\')\n    \n    if accordion_container:\n        print(f"âœ“ Found main accordion container")\n        print(f"Accordion container ID: {accordion_container.get(\'id\', \'No ID\')}")\n        \n        # Find all accordion items (li elements with accordion-item class)\n        accordion_items = accordion_container.find_all(\'li\', class_=\'accordion-item\')\n        print(f"âœ“ Found {len(accordion_items)} accordion items")\n        \n        if len(accordion_items) > 0:\n            print(f"\\n=== STEP 2: EXTRACTING ALL FLAVORS FROM ACCORDION ITEMS ===\\n")\n            \n            extracted_flavors = []\n            \n            for item_idx, item in enumerate(accordion_items, 1):\n                try:\n                    # Extract flavor name from the accordion button\n                    button = item.find(\'button\', class_=\'accordion-button\')\n                    flavor_name = button.get_text(strip=True) if button else f"Unknown Flavor {item_idx}"\n                    \n                    # Extract content from the accordion body\n                    accordion_body = item.find(\'div\', class_=\'accordion-body\')\n                    \n                    if accordion_body:\n                        # Get all text content from the body\n                        body_text = accordion_body.get_text(strip=True)\n                        \n                        # Look for date ranges using multiple patterns\n                        date_patterns = [\n                            r\'(\\d{4})[-â€“â€”](\\d{4})\',  # 1979-1991\n                            r\'(\\d{4})\\s*[-â€“â€”]\\s*(\\d{4})\',  # 1979 - 1991\n                            r\'\\b(\\d{4})\\s*[-â€“â€”]\\s*(\\d{4})\\b\',  # Word boundaries\n                        ]\n                        \n                        dates_found = []\n                        for pattern in date_patterns:\n                            matches = re.findall(pattern, body_text)\n                            if matches:\n                                dates_found.extend(matches)\n                                break  # Use first successful pattern\n                        \n                        if dates_found:\n                            # Use the first date range found\n                            start_year_str, end_year_str = dates_found[0]\n                            start_year = int(start_year_str)\n                            end_year = int(end_year_str)\n                            \n                            # Extract rhyme lines from <em> tags\n                            rhyme_elements = accordion_body.find_all(\'em\')\n                            rhyme_lines = []\n                            \n                            for em in rhyme_elements:\n                                rhyme_text = em.get_text(strip=True)\n                                if rhyme_text:\n                                    # Split by line breaks and clean up\n                                    lines = [line.strip() for line in rhyme_text.replace(\'\\n\', \'|\').split(\'|\') if line.strip()]\n                                    rhyme_lines.extend(lines)\n                            \n                            # Extract description (the paragraph between date and rhyme)\n                            content_paragraphs = accordion_body.find_all(\'p\')\n                            description = ""\n                            for p in content_paragraphs:\n                                p_text = p.get_text(strip=True)\n                                # Skip the date paragraph and rhyme paragraphs\n                                if not re.search(r\'\\d{4}[-â€“â€”]\\d{4}\', p_text) and not p.find(\'em\'):\n                                    description = p_text\n                                    break\n                            \n                            flavor_info = {\n                                \'name\': flavor_name,\n                                \'start_year\': start_year,\n                                \'end_year\': end_year,\n                                \'date_range\': f\'{start_year}-{end_year}\',\n                                \'earliest_year\': start_year,\n                                \'description\': description,\n                                \'rhyme_lines\': rhyme_lines,\n                                \'last_rhyme_line\': rhyme_lines[-1] if rhyme_lines else None\n                            }\n                            \n                            extracted_flavors.append(flavor_info)\n                            \n                            print(f"{item_idx:2d}. {flavor_name} ({start_year}-{end_year})")\n                            if rhyme_lines:\n                                print(f"     Rhyme lines: {len(rhyme_lines)}")\n                                print(f"     Last line: {rhyme_lines[-1]}")\n                            print(f"     Description: {description[:100]}{\'...\' if len(description) > 100 else \'\'}")\n                        \n                        else:\n                            print(f"{item_idx:2d}. {flavor_name} - No date range found")\n                            print(f"     Body text preview: {body_text[:100]}...")\n                    \n                    else:\n                        print(f"{item_idx:2d}. {flavor_name} - No accordion body found")\n                \n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f"{item_idx:2d}. Error processing item: {e}")\n                    continue\n            \n            # Sort by earliest year to find the true oldest flavor\n            if extracted_flavors:\n                extracted_flavors.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'earliest_year\'])\n                \n                print(f"\\n=== STEP 3: ALL FLAVORS SORTED BY AGE ===\\n")\n                print(f"Total flavors extracted: {len(extracted_flavors)}")\n                \n                print(f"\\nComplete list of flavors sorted by earliest year:")\n                for i, flavor in enumerate(extracted_flavors, 1):\n                    print(f"{i:2d}. {flavor[\'name\']} ({flavor[\'date_range\']}) - Started: {flavor[\'earliest_year\']}")\n                    if flavor.get(\'last_rhyme_line\'):\n                        print(f"     Last rhyme line: {flavor[\'last_rhyme_line\']}")\n                \n                # Identify the true oldest flavor\n                oldest_flavor = extracted_flavors[0]\n                print(f"\\nðŸŽ¯ TRUE OLDEST BEN & JERRY\'S FLAVOR IDENTIFIED:")\n                print(f"   Name: {oldest_flavor[\'name\']}")\n                print(f"   Date Range: {oldest_flavor[\'date_range\']}")\n                print(f"   Started: {oldest_flavor[\'earliest_year\']}")\n                print(f"   Description: {oldest_flavor.get(\'description\', \'No description\')}")\n                if oldest_flavor.get(\'rhyme_lines\'):\n                    print(f"   Rhyme lines: {len(oldest_flavor[\'rhyme_lines\'])}")\n                    for i, line in enumerate(oldest_flavor[\'rhyme_lines\'], 1):\n                        print(f"     {i}. {line}")\n                    print(f"   *** LAST RHYME LINE: {oldest_flavor[\'last_rhyme_line\']} ***")\n                \n                print(f"\\n=== STEP 4: FINDING HEADSTONE IMAGE FOR OLDEST FLAVOR ===\\n")\n                \n                # Look for headstone images in the HTML\n                all_images = soup.find_all(\'img\')\n                headstone_images = []\n                \n                for img in all_images:\n                    img_src = img.get(\'src\', \'\') or img.get(\'data-src\', \'\')\n                    img_alt = img.get(\'alt\', \'\')\n                    \n                    if img_src and (\'graveyard\' in img_src.lower() or \'tombstone\' in img_alt.lower()):\n                        # Convert relative URLs to absolute\n                        if img_src.startswith(\'//\'):\n                            img_src = \'https:\' + img_src\n                        elif img_src.startswith(\'/\'):\n                            img_src = \'https://www.benjerry.com\' + img_src\n                        elif not img_src.startswith(\'http\'):\n                            img_src = \'https://www.benjerry.com/\' + img_src\n                        \n                        headstone_images.append({\n                            \'src\': img_src,\n                            \'alt\': img_alt,\n                            \'context\': \'graveyard_headstone\'\n                        })\n                \n                print(f"Found {len(headstone_images)} headstone images")\n                \n                # Match the oldest flavor with its headstone image\n                oldest_flavor_name = oldest_flavor[\'name\'].lower()\n                matching_images = []\n                \n                for img in headstone_images:\n                    img_alt = img.get(\'alt\', \'\').lower()\n                    img_src = img.get(\'src\', \'\').lower()\n                    \n                    # Check for word matches\n                    flavor_words = oldest_flavor_name.split()\n                    matches = 0\n                    \n                    for word in flavor_words:\n                        if len(word) > 3:  # Skip short words\n                            if word in img_alt or word in img_src:\n                                matches += 1\n                    \n                    if matches > 0:\n                        img_copy = img.copy()\n                        img_copy[\'match_score\'] = matches\n                        matching_images.append(img_copy)\n                \n                if matching_images:\n                    # Sort by match score\n                    matching_images.sort(key=lambda x: x.get(\'match_score\', 0), reverse=True)\n                    \n                    best_match = matching_images[0]\n                    print(f"\\nâœ“ OLDEST FLAVOR HEADSTONE IMAGE LOCATED:")\n                    print(f"   Flavor: {oldest_flavor[\'name\']}")\n                    print(f"   Alt text: {best_match.get(\'alt\', \'No alt text\')}")\n                    print(f"   URL: {best_match.get(\'src\', \'No URL\')}")\n                    print(f"   Match score: {best_match.get(\'match_score\', 0)}")\n                    \n                    # Save comprehensive final results\n                    final_results = {\n                        \'analysis_date\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                        \'extraction_method\': \'direct_html_accordion_parsing\',\n                        \'total_flavors_extracted\': len(extracted_flavors),\n                        \'oldest_flavor\': oldest_flavor,\n                        \'oldest_flavor_headstone_image\': best_match,\n                        \'all_flavors_complete_list\': extracted_flavors,\n                        \'plan_progress\': {\n                            \'phase_1_complete\': True,\n                            \'oldest_flavor_identified\': oldest_flavor[\'name\'],\n                            \'oldest_flavor_years\': oldest_flavor[\'date_range\'],\n                            \'headstone_image_url\': best_match.get(\'src\', \'No URL\'),\n                            \'next_phase\': \'Download headstone image and analyze background\'\n                        }\n                    }\n                    \n                    results_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'ben_jerrys_complete_graveyard_analysis.json\')\n                    with open(results_file, \'w\') as f:\n                        json.dump(final_results, f, indent=2)\n                    \n                    print(f"\\nâœ“ Complete analysis saved to: {results_file}")\n                    \n                    print(f"\\n=== PLAN PHASE 1 SUCCESSFULLY COMPLETED ===\\n")\n                    print(f"ðŸŽ¯ OLDEST BEN & JERRY\'S FLAVOR: {oldest_flavor[\'name\']} ({oldest_flavor[\'date_range\']})")\n                    print(f"ðŸ“¸ HEADSTONE IMAGE URL: {best_match.get(\'src\', \'No URL\')}")\n                    if oldest_flavor.get(\'last_rhyme_line\'):\n                        print(f"ðŸ“ OLDEST FLAVOR\'S LAST RHYME LINE: {oldest_flavor[\'last_rhyme_line\']}")\n                    \n                    print(f"\\nðŸ“‹ READY FOR PLAN PHASE 2:")\n                    print(f"   1. Download the oldest flavor\'s headstone image")\n                    print(f"   2. Examine the photo for background headstones")\n                    print(f"   3. Extract flavor name and rhyme from background headstone")\n                    print(f"   4. First check file size and structure\n    file_size = os.path.getsize(analysis_file)\n    print(f"Analysis file size: {file_size:,} bytes")\n    \n    with open(analysis_file, \'r\') as f:\n        content_preview = f.read(500)  # Read first 500 characters to check structure\n        print(f"File content preview: {content_preview}...")\n    \n    # Now safely load and inspect the JSON structure\n    try:\n        with open(analysis_file, \'r\') as f:\n            analysis_data = json.load(f)\n        \n        print("\\nAnalysis file structure:")\n        for key, value in analysis_data.items():\n            if isinstance(value, list):\n                print(f"  {key}: List with {len(value)} items")\n            elif isinstance(value, dict):\n                print(f"  {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys")\n            else:\n                print(f"  {key}: {value}")\n        \n        #
